(this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) The budget session of Parliament is going to start on Tuesday, 23 February
 2016-17 kaa aam bajet loksabhaa main agle somvaar, 29 farvari ko pesh kiya jayega
 Meanwhile, while the North Block (ministry of Finance) has been keeping traditional secrecy in the preparations for the budget, this year is the first time that the secretaries in the Ministry of Finance have used youtube to indicate the direction of the General Budget 2016-17
 Have recourse apane khud ke you-tub channel kaa upyog karte hue mantralay ne bajet kaa mahatv darshaya hai
 The ministry has also demonstrated the pattern of carrying the budget papers in a leather briefcase by the finance minister to present the budget
 aamtaur par bajet kii taiyaari main lagi north block ke sambandhit hisse main janvari ke shuru se hi patrakaron evam aam janata kaa pravesh band kar diya jaataa he
 With this, everything coming in and going out of North Block is subjected to special X-ray scans and it is monitored closely
 saath hi shaktishaalee mobile phone jaimar yantra laga die jate hai, taaki mobile phone kol se kisi soochna ko baahar na kiya ja sake
 Internet connections are closed in the offices of senior officers and employees involved in the process, and the budget branch of North Block functions as a war room
 loksabhaa main bajet pesh hone tak north block main suraksha ke ucchtam str ke upaay lagu rahete hai
 The Security Office (IB), Delhi Police and CISF are all involved in the security of the region
 is baar bajet kii taiyaari kaa antim charan shuukravaar ko halava samaaroh ke saath shuru ho gaya
 In this, the process of printing the documents of the general budget begins
 is samaaroh main koi puja-archana nahin hoti
 Jaitley and the officials involved with the preparations for this budget gathered in the printing press located in the basement of North Block and distributed halwa, greeting each other
 iske saath hi bajet ke din ke liye ulti ginati shuru ho gai
 The budget is usually presented on the last day of February and the last day of February this year is falling on 29 February, Monday
 iske kuch saptaah baad pashchim bengal, kerala or assam jaise rajyon main vidhansabha chunaav hone hai
 All these documents are protected by a 'blue jacket'
 ise nila jacket isliye bhi kehete hai, kyonki isamen bajet ke liye mahatvapurn sankhya hote hai
 The joint secretary (budget) of the ministry is in charge of this and does not let anyone, even the finance minister, take it out of the North Block
 bajet banane kii sampurna prakriya ke dauraan mantralay ke kuch hi adhikari is dastavej ko dekh pate hai
 The Finance Minister's speech is prepared a few hours before the Budget is presented
 is baar kaa bajet is lihaaj se ahm he ki jetali ko vruddhi dar main teji lani he or desh main kam nivesh ko lekar aa rahi samasyaon kaa samaadhaan karnaa he
 Along with this, they also have the responsibility to control the fiscal deficit and revenue deficit
 simit sansadhano ke saath jetali par madhyam varg ko khush rakhane evam krishi va dhanchaagat jaise kshetron ke muddon kaa samaadhaan karne kaa bhi jimmaa he
 Many are not expecting major announcements in the budget, but a framework is expected to be introduced for economic reforms, especially on the tax front, to restore investor confidence
 varsh 1947 (jab 26 november, 1947 ko pehla bajet pesh kiya gaya tha) se lekar 1950 tak bajet dastavej kii chapai raashtrapati bhawan main hua karti thi, lekin 1950 main bajet li hone ke baad chapai kaa sthaan badalakar minto road sthit ek sarkaar press kar diya gaya
 The comments haalanki, 1980 se north block kaa basament chapai ke liye ek sthaayee jagah ban gaya he
 This budget press is fully air conditioned and equipped with modern printing machines
 halava samaaroh ke baad 100 karmchaariyon ko north block ke basament main le jaaya jaataa he, jahaan do printing press hai
 There they are kept till the entire process is completed and no outsider can contact them
 ye log chapai, pruf reeding or anuwaad ke kaam main shaamil hote hai
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Using its own youtube channel, the Ministry has shown the importance of the budget
 mantralay ne bajet ko prastut karne ke liye vitt mantri dwaara bajet patron ko chamade ke ek brifces main le jane kii paripati ko bhi pradarshit kiya he
 Generally, the entry of journalists and general public in the concerned part of the North Block, which is preparing for the budget, is stopped from the beginning of January
 iske saath hi north block main aane vaali or yahaan se baahar jane vaali har cheez ko vishesh eks-re scan se guzaar kar us par paini najar rakhi jaataa he
 Also, powerful mobile phone jammer devices are installed, so that no information can be excluded from mobile phone calls
 varisht adhikariyon or prakriya main shaamil karmchaariyon ke karyaalayon main internet conection band kar die jate hai or north block kii bajet shakha ek waar-room kii tarah kaam karne lagati he
 The highest level of security measures in North Block remain in force until the budget is presented in the Lok Sabha
 is kshetra kii suraksha main khufia karyaalay (ibi), dilli police or siaisef sabhi shaamil rahete hai
 This time the final phase of budget preparation started on Friday with the pudding ceremony
 isamen aam bajet ke dastavejon kii chapai kii prakriya shuru hoti he
 There is no worship in this ceremony
 jetali or is bajet kii taiyaariyon se jude adhikari north block ke basament main sthit printing press main ekatra hue or ek-duusare ko shubhakamanaayen dete hue halava baanta
 With this, the countdown for the budget day started
 bajet aamtaur par farvari ke antim din pesh kiya jaataa he or is saal farvari kaa aakhri din 29 farvari, somvaar ko pad rahaa he
 a few weeks later, assembly elections are due in states like West Bengal, Kerala and Assam
 in sabhi dastavejon kii suraksha ek 'nila jacket' karata he
 It is also called blue jacket because it contains significant numbers for the budget
 mantralay kaa sanyukt sachiv (bajet) iskaa prabharee hota he or vah kisi ko bhi yahaan tak ki vitt mantri ko bhi ise north block se baahar le jane nahin detaa
 During the entire budget-making process, only a few officers of the Ministry are able to see this document
 vitt mantri kaa bhaashan, bajet pesh hone se kuch ghante pehle hi taiyaar kiya jaataa he
 This time budget is important in the sense that Jaitley has to accelerate the growth rate and solve the problems of low investment in the country
 iske saath hi un par rajkoshiya ghaataa or rajasav ghate par bhi niyantran karne kii jimmedaari he
 With limited resources, Jaitley is also tasked with keeping the middle class happy and addressing issues in areas such as agriculture and infrastructure
 kai log bajet main badi ghoshnaaon kii ummid nahin kar rahe hai, lekin aarthik sudhaaron ke liye visheshkar tex ke morche par ek ruparekha pesh kiye jane kii ummid jarur he, jisase niveshkon kaa vishwaas behaal kiya ja sake
 From 1947 (when the first budget was presented on November 26, 1947) to 1950, the printing of the budget document was done in Rashtrapati Bhavan, but after the budget was leaked in 1950, the printing of the government was changed to a government press tax on Minto Road
 Given
 tippaniyan However, since 1980 the North Block's basement has become a permanent place for printing
 yah bajet press purna vaataanukoolit he or aadhunik printing mashiinon se las he
 After the pudding ceremony, 100 employees are taken to the basement of the North Block, where there are two printing presses
 vahaan unhen sampurna prakriya puri hone tak rakhaa jaataa he or koi bhi bahari vyakti unase sampark nahin kar saktaa
 These people are involved in printing, proof reading and translation work

 Taught in English as 'goal Management', there are five points in this lesson, whose first English letter has a familiar word 'smart' - SMART
 
 
 • es, yani spacific, yani vishisht, yani vishesh rup se kendrit
 
 
 • M, ie measurable, which can be measured
 
 
 • e, yani achivable, yani jo hasil kiya ja saktaa ho, yani uplabdh sansadhano main saadhy ho
 
 
 R, ie Reliable, ie reliable
 
 
 • tii, yani time bound, yani samaybaddh ho
 
 
 The promises of the Election Manifestos of Bihar can be easily tested with the help of these five points considering the declared targets of those parties
 smart gol kaa yah formula desh ke kam se kam 10 karod yuvaaon, jinamein chah karod shikshit yuva, jo sammanjanak rojgaar ke liye line lagaakar khadey ho gaye hai, unke jaanane-samajhane ke kaam aa saktaa he
 This formula will also be useful for reviewing the work done till date in the country that was being built after independence
 itnaa hi nahin, lakshya prabandhan kaa yah formula har saal do karod kii raftaar se bad rahi jansankhya ke kaaran nikat bhavishya main munhabaae khadin teen pramukh chunautiyon - berogari, jal sankat or aakasmik aapadaaon - se nipatane kii yojana banane ke kaam bhi aa saktaa he

 in tathyon ke aadhaar par bihar ke chunavi ghoshnapatron ko jaanchen to ye sabhi baaten vishisht lakshya ke paimaane par nahin dikhaai deteen

 ' The main festival of Indians, Makar Sankranti is celebrated in different states, cities and villages according to the traditions there
 isi din se alag-alag rajyon main ganga nadi ke kinare magh mela yaa ganga snaan kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he
 The first bath of Kumbh also begins on this day
 makar sankranti kya he?surya ke ek raashi se duusari raashi main jane ko hi sankranti kehete hai
 The time between one solstice to another is the solar month
 vaise to surya sankranti 12 hai, lekin inamen se chaar sankranti mahatvapurn hai jinamein mesh, kark, tula, makar sankranti hai
 Bathing in the auspicious time of Makar Sankranti, the auspicious time of charity and virtue have special significance
 makar sankranti ke paavan parv par gud or til lagaakar narmada main snaan karnaa laabhadaayi hota he
 After this, donating jaggery, oil, blanket, fruit, umbrella etc
 in Dan Sankranti gives benefits and results in virtue
 14 janvari aisa din he, jab dharti par achche din kii shuruyaat hoti he
 This is because the sun starts moving north instead of south
 jab tak surya purv se dakshin kii ore gaman karata he tab tak uski kirnon kaa asar kharaab mana gaya he, lekin jab vah purv se uttar kii ore gaman karte lagata he tab uski kirane sehat or shanti ko badhaati hai
 Makar Sankranti festival is celebrated by different names in different states
 uttar pradesh : makar sankranti ko khichdi parv kaha jaataa he
 The Sun is worshiped
 chaaval or daal kii khichdi khai or daan kii jaati he
 Gujarat and Rajasthan: Celebrated as Uttarayan festival
 patang utsav kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he
 Andhra Pradesh: a three-day festival known as Sankranti
 tamilnadu : kisaanon kaa ye pramukh parv pongal ke naam se manaaya jaataa he
 Dal-rice khichdi is cooked and fed in ghee
 maharashtra : log gajak or til ke laddu khate hai or ek duusare ko bhent dekar shubhakamanaayen dete hai
 West Bengal: Ganga Sagar Mela is organized on the Hooghly River
 assam : bhogali bihu ke naam se is parv ko manaaya jaataa he
 Punjab: a day earlier is celebrated as Lohri festival
 dhoomdhaam ke saath samarohon kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he
 Nava forms of Shakti are worshiped in Navratri
 raatri shabd siddhi kaa pratik he
 More than days are given importance for worship and siddhis
 hindu ke adhiktar parv ratriyon main hi manaaye jate hai
 Among the festivals celebrated at night are Deepavali, Holika Dussehra etc
 shivaratri or navaratri bhi inamen se ek hai
 Navratri Special: up's CM Yogis perform difficult austerities, give up, and in Annahindu festivals, the festivals which are celebrated in the night of the night, especially in those festivals, the attainment of accomplishment is specially done
 navaratri ke saath raatri jodne kaa bhi yahi arth he ki mata shakti ke in nau dinon kii ratriyon ko manan va chintan ke liye prayog karnaa chahie
 In Navratri, people do many types of fasting, abstinence, rules, bhajans, worship yoga, etc
 to increase their spiritual and mental powers
 navaratri ke shubh dinon main bhuulakar bhi na karen ye kaamakyon karen maa kii upasnavarsh main do baar avashya navaratri main maa durga kii upasna kerani chahie, isse maa kaa vishesh aashirwad miltaa he or dukh dur hote hai
 At the beginning of the year, nine days from the Pratipada of Shukla Paksha in Chaitra month, that is, Navami and similarly, after six months Ashwin month, from Pratipada of Shukla Paksha to worship one day before Vijayadashami
 caitra navaratri shuru, jaane kalash sthapana kaa shubh muhuurtanavaraatri main raat main kyon kare pujapathrishiyon ne raatri ko adhik mahatv diya he
 From the scientific side, we try to understand this fact
 raatri main purna shaanti hoti he
 The transgressions go awry
 man-dhyaan ko ekagra karnaa saral hota he

 shant vaataavaran main mantron kaa jaap vishesh laabh detaa he

 is samay ko aatmasakti or maansik shakti kii prapti ke liye saralata se upyog kiya ja saktaa he

 pani kii killat ke bich bhoojal sroton or nadiyon ne desh ke niti nirmaataaon kaa bharpoor dhyaan khinchaa he
 These water sources are now on the radar
 sadiyon se jhilein, talab, baawali samet anya prakritik or maanav nirmit jal strot pine ke liye, gharelu upyog or krishi ke liye pani uplabdh kara rahe hai
 These waters raise the ground water level
 saath hi shaharon main baadh kii ashanka ko kam karte hai
 Encroachment on such water bodies has led to flash floods in many cities
 pichley dedh dashak ke dauraan 2005 main mumbai, 2013 main uttarakhand, 2014 main jammu-kashmir or 2015 main chennai aise hi flash flud kaa shikaar hue hai
 If we pay attention to the recommendations of NITI Aayog, more emphasis needs to be given to the revival and management of water resources
 kyonki dilli, hyderabad or bengaluru samet desh ke 21 bade shaharon main saal 2020 tak bhoojal khatm ho jayega
 This will affect 100 million people
 aniyantrit shaharikaran kii vajah se shaharon or gaanvon se jalstrot teji se khatm ho rahe hai
 We also see it day by day and read it in various research reports
 jalsroton ke bure haal kaa sabase bada kaaran atikaraman, kachra damp, sivarej, audyogic kachra, nirmansthal se nikalne vaala malba or pani ke saamudayik upyog se vyaktigat upyog kii taraf badhanaa he
 Rapidly disappearing watersheds are disappearing rapidly from different states of the country
 tisare miner irigation (MI) sensos 2000-01 ke anusaar desh main 556,601 jalstrot the, jo 2006-07 main hue chauthe miner irigation (MI) sensos main ghatakar 523,816 jalstrot ho gaye
 That means 32,785 water sources decreased
 in 523,816 jalsroton main 80,128 (15%) jalstrot kisi upyog ke liye nahin bache
 Such sources are more in Karnataka, Rajasthan, Andhra Pradesh, Tamil Nadu, Uttarakhand and Gujarat
 miner irigation (MI) sensos puure desh kii sahi tasviir nahin dikhaata kyonki yah sirf gramin ilaakon tak hi simit he
 The fifth Minor Irrigation (MI) census was held in 2013–14 but the data of the watershed was not released
 miner irigation (MI) sensos main ek khami yah bhi he ki rajyon ke sabhi jalsroton ke aankaden to hai lekin yah nahin pataa chalata he ki koun sa jalstrot upyog main kyon nahin he
 Also, it has not been told which source of damage has been caused and why
 is vajah se jalsroton ke punarutthan kaa kaam nahin ho paa rahaa he
 The Parliamentary Standing Committee on Water Resources has prepared two reports on urban and rural areas in 2016 and 2017
 isamen jalsroton ko lekar rajya sarkaron se kai sawaal kiye the, lekin rajya sarkaron ne centre ko koi jawaab nahin diya
 Because of this, the Sixth Minor Irrigation (MI) census to be held in 2019-20 is not being started
 rajya sarkaron ke is ravaiye se naaraaz jal sansaadhan sambandhi sansadeey sthaayee samiti ne kaha ki desh main tatkaal jalsroton ko lekar survey karaane kii zarurat he
 If this is not done soon, it will be difficult to find solutions to the problems arising with the watershed
 jal sansaadhan mantralay ne bhi kam ho rahe jalsroton par chintaa jaahir kii thi
 The number of all the sources in the country is known through satellite mapping
 lekin jal sansaadhan sambandhi sansadeey sthaayee samiti ne yah chintaa jataai he ki jalsroton kii sankhya or unke upyogon kii ginati kisi kaam kii nahin he, jab tak inke aadhaar par samaadhaan na khoje jaaen
 Repair, Renovation and Restoration Scheme for Water Resources In 2005, the Center launched the Repair, Renovation and Restoration (RRR) scheme for water resources
 isamen sangrahan kshamta, bhoojal or peyajal badhaane kii yojana banaai gai thi
 This included conserving traditional watersheds, increasing their water level, increasing tank storage capacity, increasing groundwater levels, etc
 lekin jal sansaadhan sambandhi sansadeey sthaayee samiti ne jalsroton ke bure haal par aapatti jataane ke baad repere, rinovations or restauration (RRR) skim par dobaaraa najar daalane kii jarurat he
 According to the United Nations World Water Development Report 2018, all the countries of the world had appealed to save the natural waters by adopting traditional methods
 isamen do bade udhaaharan die gaye the
 The first is the plan of Rajendra Singh, called Waterman of India in Alwar district of Rajasthan
 jisamen unhone 1000 suukhaagrast gaanvon main chote-chote rain water harvesting dhaanche banaakar pani kaa str badhaayaa
 Due to this, the agricultural yield of these villages increased by 20 to 80 percent
 saath hi 33 fisadi jangal bhi bad gaye
 The second example was of Jordan
 jahaan paaramparik jameen prabandhan system hima shuru kiya gaya he
 Here the land was left on its natural condition so that it could improve on its own
 saath hi aise paudhe lagaae gaye jo aarthik rup se desh ke majboot kar rahe hai
 Jordan applied the same formula to save the natural resources of the Zarqa River Basin
 desh main kai aisi yojanaayen hai jo paaramparik jal prabandhan ko badhaava dete hai lekin repere, rinovations or restauration (RRR) skim se aisa bilkul nahin hota
 The Parliamentary Standing Committee on Water Resources had said that new water resources should also be created through the RRR scheme so that the shortage of old water resources that are running out can be met
 madhyapradesh, telugana, arunachal pradesh, rajasthan, mizoram, tripura or odisha jaise rajyon ne manaregaa jaisi yojanaon ke tahat nae tanks, check dam jaise jalstrot banaae hai
 But the Ministry of Water Resources rejected the recommendation of the parliamentary committee
 ab yah dekhnaa hoga ki kaise hamen jalsroton ko bachaana he, taaki bhavishya main hone vaali pani kii killat se agali peedi ko bachaaya ja sake
